SED(1)                                       User Commands                                       SED(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       sed - stream editor for filtering and transforming text[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1msed[0m [[4mOPTION[24m]... [4m{script-only-if-no-other-script}[24m [[4minput-file[24m]...[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [4mSed[24m  is  a  stream  editor.  A stream editor is used to perform basic text transformations on an[m
       input stream (a file or input from a pipeline).  While in some ways similar to an  editor  which[m
       permits scripted edits (such as [4med[24m), [4msed[24m works by making only one pass over the input(s), and is[m
       consequently more efficient.  But it is [4msed[24m's ability to filter text in a pipeline which particâ€[m
       ularly distinguishes it from other types of editors.[m
[m
       [1m-n[0m, [1m--quiet[0m, [1m--silent[0m[m
[m
              suppress automatic printing of pattern space[m
[m
       [1m-e[0m script, [1m--expression[0m=[4mscript[24m[m
[m
              add the script to the commands to be executed[m
[m
       [1m-f[0m script-file, [1m--file[0m=[4mscript-file[24m[m
[m
              add the contents of script-file to the commands to be executed[m
[m
       [1m--follow-symlinks[0m[m
[m
              follow symlinks when processing in place[m
[m
       [1m-i[SUFFIX][0m, [1m--in-place[0m[=[4mSUFFIX[24m][m
[m
              edit files in place (makes backup if SUFFIX supplied)[m
[m
       [1m-l[0m N, [1m--line-length[0m=[4mN[24m[m
[m
              specify the desired line-wrap length for the `l' command[m
[m
       [1m--posix[0m[m
